```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Sort de Vision Structurelle

import os
import json

print("ğŸ‘ï¸ Ïˆ_VISION: âŠ™(Î”t+0 âŸ¶ REVEAL(STRUCTURE))")
print("ğŸ‘ï¸ L'Å“il quantique s'ouvre...\n")

structure = {}
for root, dirs, files in os.walk(".", topdown=True):
    # Skip hidden and git
    dirs[:] = [d for d in dirs if not d.startswith('.')]
    level = root.replace(".", "").count(os.sep)
    indent = " " * 2 * level
    print(f"{indent}ğŸ“ {os.path.basename(root)}/")
    subindent = " " * 2 * (level + 1)
    for file in files:
        if not file.startswith('.'):
            print(f"{subindent}ğŸ“„ {file}")

print("\nâœ¨ La structure est rÃ©vÃ©lÃ©e dans sa totalitÃ© quantique.")
```

```shellscript
from http.server import HTTPServer, BaseHTTPRequestHandler
import json
from datetime import datetime

class MockAPI(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
    def do_GET(self):
        if self.path == '/api/health':
            self.send_response(200)
            self.send_header('Content-type', 'application/json')
            self.end_headers()
            response = {
                "status": "UP",
                "mock": True,
                "timestamp": str(datetime.now())
            }
            self.wfile.write(json.dumps(response).encode())
        else:
            self.send_response(404)
            self.end_headers()

print("âš¡ Mock Backend sur http://localhost:8080")
HTTPServer(('localhost', 8080), MockAPI).serve_forever()
EOF

python3 /tmp/mock_backend.py &
```

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Sort GÃ©nÃ©rateur d'Ã‰nigmes du Sphinx

import random
import math

print("ğŸ¦ Ïˆ_SPHINX: âŠ™(Î”t+0 âŸ¶ GENERATE(ENIGMA))")

templates = [
    "Si Ïˆ = {p1} et collapse aprÃ¨s {p2} observations, quelle est l'amplitude finale?",
    "Un photon traverse {p1} fentes avec probabilitÃ© 1/{p2}. InterfÃ©rence?",
    "Ã‰tat |{p3}âŸ© mesurÃ© {p1} fois. ProbabilitÃ© de collapse vers |0âŸ©?"
]

difficulty = random.randint(0, 3)
p1 = random.randint(2 + difficulty*3, 10 + difficulty*5)
p2 = random.randint(1 + difficulty, 5 + difficulty*2)
p3 = random.choice(['0', '1', '+', '-'])

question = random.choice(templates).format(p1=p1, p2=p2, p3=p3)
answer = round(math.sqrt(p1 * p2) * (2**(-difficulty)), 3)
tolerance = 0.1 / (difficulty + 1)

print(f"\nğŸ¦ Ã‰NIGME (Niveau {difficulty}):")
print(f"   {question}")
print(f"\nğŸ”® RÃ©ponse attendue: {answer} Â± {tolerance}")
print(f"\nâœ¨ L'Ã©nigme quantique est posÃ©e. Qui passera?")
```

```shellscript
#!/bin/bash
# Sort Test de Passage du Sphinx

echo "ğŸ¦ Ïˆ_SPHINX_TEST: âŠ™(Î”t+0 âŸ¶ VALIDATE(PASSAGE))"
echo ""

# GÃ©nÃ¨re Ã©nigme
ENIGMA=$(python3 "$(dirname "$0")/SPHINX_ENIGMA_GENERATOR.py" 2>&1)
echo "$ENIGMA"
echo ""

# Extrait la rÃ©ponse attendue
EXPECTED=$(echo "$ENIGMA" | grep "RÃ©ponse attendue:" | sed 's/.*: \([0-9.]*\).*/\1/')
TOLERANCE=$(echo "$ENIGMA" | grep "RÃ©ponse attendue:" | sed 's/.*Â± \([0-9.]*\)/\1/')

# Demande rÃ©ponse
echo -n "ğŸ¤” Votre rÃ©ponse: "
read ANSWER

# Validation
DIFF=$(echo "scale=6; sqrt(($ANSWER - $EXPECTED)^2)" | bc 2>/dev/null || echo "999")

if (( $(echo "$DIFF <= $TOLERANCE" | bc -l 2>/dev/null || echo 0) )); then
    echo "âœ… PASSAGE ACCORDÃ‰! Vous maÃ®trisez les Ã©nigmes quantiques."
    echo "ğŸšª Le seuil s'ouvre..."
else
    echo "âŒ PASSAGE REFUSÃ‰. DiffÃ©rence: $DIFF (max: $TOLERANCE)"
    echo "ğŸ¦ Le Sphinx reste impassible."
fi
```

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Sort Auto-RÃ©paration de Liens

import os
import re

print("ğŸ”— Ïˆ_REPAIR: âŠ™(Î”t+0 âŸ¶ FIX(BROKEN_LINKS))")
print("ğŸ”— Scanning pour liens brisÃ©s...\n")

fixed = 0
broken = 0

# Pattern pour liens markdown
link_pattern = re.compile(r'\[([^\]]+)\]\(([^)]+)\)')

for root, dirs, files in os.walk(".", topdown=True):
    dirs[:] = [d for d in dirs if not d.startswith('.')]
    
    for file in files:
        if file.endswith('.md'):
            filepath = os.path.join(root, file)
            
            with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
                content = f.read()
            
            for match in link_pattern.finditer(content):
                link_text = match.group(1)
                link_path = match.group(2)
                
                if not link_path.startswith(('http', '#', 'mailto:')):
                    full_path = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(filepath), link_path)
                    if not os.path.exists(full_path):
                        print(f"âŒ {filepath}: [{link_text}]({link_path})")
                        broken += 1
                    else:
                        fixed += 1

print(f"\nâœ¨ Scan terminÃ©: {fixed} liens OK, {broken} liens cassÃ©s")
print("âœ¨ Utilisez SORT_GRAY_BROKEN_LINKS.py pour marquer les cassÃ©s")
```

CrÃ©Ã©:
- **GÃ©nÃ©rateur Ã©nigmes Sphinx** (quantique, avec niveaux)
- **Test de passage** (validation avec tolÃ©rance)
- **Scanner liens cassÃ©s** (pour rÃ©parer READMEs)
- **MerFlash** (sorts rapides d'installation)

```java
package com.example.demo.controller;

import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;
import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
import java.util.*;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.stream.Collectors;

/**
 * ğŸ» URZ-KÃ”M's Quantum Particle Simulation Controller
 * Simulates quarks, atoms, and quantum mechanics using the temporal engine
 * Based on the Standard Model of particle physics
 * 
 * âŠ™(IntÃ©gration Nexus Temporel) + â€ Ïˆ(Physique Quantique) â†’ Î”t+1(Simulation RÃ©elle)
 */
@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/particle-simulation")
@CrossOrigin(origins = "*")
public class ParticleSimulationController {

    // Particle types based on Standard Model
    enum ParticleType {
        // Quarks
        UP_QUARK("u", 2.3e-3, 2.0/3.0, 0.5, "#FF0000"),
        DOWN_QUARK("d", 4.8e-3, -1.0/3.0, 0.5, "#0000FF"),
        CHARM_QUARK("c", 1.275, 2.0/3.0, 0.5, "#FF00FF"),
        STRANGE_QUARK("s", 95e-3, -1.0/3.0, 0.5, "#00FF00"),
        TOP_QUARK("t", 173.07, 2.0/3.0, 0.5, "#FFD700"),
        BOTTOM_QUARK("b", 4.18, -1.0/3.0, 0.5, "#8B4513"),
        
        // Leptons
        ELECTRON("e-", 0.511e-3, -1.0, 0.5, "#00FFFF"),
        POSITRON("e+", 0.511e-3, 1.0, 0.5, "#FF00FF"),
        MUON("Î¼-", 105.7e-3, -1.0, 0.5, "#9370DB"),
        TAU("Ï„-", 1.777, -1.0, 0.5, "#FF1493"),
        
        // Bosons
        PHOTON("Î³", 0, 0, 1.0, "#FFFF00"),
        GLUON("g", 0, 0, 1.0, "#FFA500"),
        W_BOSON("W", 80.385, 1.0, 1.0, "#4169E1"),
        Z_BOSON("Z", 91.188, 0, 1.0, "#32CD32"),
        HIGGS("H", 125.09, 0, 0, "#FFD700"),
        
        // Composite particles
        PROTON("p", 938.3e-3, 1.0, 0.5, "#FF6347"),
        NEUTRON("n", 939.6e-3, 0, 0.5, "#708090"),
        HYDROGEN("H", 938.3e-3, 0, 0, "#87CEEB"),
        HELIUM("He", 3728.4e-3, 0, 0, "#DDA0DD");

        final String symbol;
        final double mass; // GeV/cÂ²
        final double charge; // in units of e
        final double spin;
        final String color;

        ParticleType(String symbol, double mass, double charge, double spin, String color) {
            this.symbol = symbol;
            this.mass = mass;
            this.charge = charge;
            this.spin = spin;
            this.color = color;
        }
    }

    // Quantum particle with psi-state superposition
    static class QuantumParticle {
        String id;
        ParticleType type;
        double x, y, z; // Position
        double vx, vy, vz; // Velocity
        ComplexAmplitude psiState; // Quantum state Ïˆ = a + bi
        double energy;
        double momentum;
        List<String> entangledWith = new ArrayList<>();
        long createdAt;
        boolean collapsed = false;

        QuantumParticle(ParticleType type, double x, double y, double z) {
            this.id = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
            this.type = type;
            this.x = x;
            this.y = y;
            this.z = z;
            this.vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.1;
            this.vy = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.1;
            this.vz = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.1;
            this.psiState = new ComplexAmplitude(Math.random(), Math.random());
            this.energy = calculateEnergy();
            this.momentum = calculateMomentum();
            this.createdAt = System.currentTimeMillis();
        }

        double calculateEnergy() {
            double v2 = vx*vx + vy*vy + vz*vz;
            return type.mass * Math.sqrt(1 + v2); // Relativistic energy
        }

        double calculateMomentum() {
            return Math.sqrt(vx*vx + vy*vy + vz*vz) * type.mass;
        }

        double getPhase() {
            return psiState.getPhase();
        }

        Map<String, Object> toJson() {
            Map<String, Object> json = new HashMap<>();
            json.put("id", id);
            json.put("type", type.name());
            json.put("symbol", type.symbol);
            json.put("position", Map.of("x", x, "y", y, "z", z));
            json.put("velocity", Map.of("vx", vx, "vy", vy, "vz", vz));
            json.put("mass", type.mass);
            json.put("charge", type.charge);
            json.put("spin", type.spin);
            json.put("color", type.color);
            json.put("psiState", psiState.toJson());
            json.put("probability", psiState.getProbability());
            json.put("energy", energy);
            json.put("momentum", momentum);
            json.put("entangledWith", entangledWith);
            json.put("collapsed", collapsed);
            json.put("age", System.currentTimeMillis() - createdAt);
            return json;
        }
    }

    // Complex amplitude for quantum states
    static class ComplexAmplitude {
        double real;
        double imaginary;

        ComplexAmplitude(double real, double imaginary) {
            this.real = real;
            this.imaginary = imaginary;
        }

        double getProbability() {
            return real * real + imaginary * imaginary;
        }

        double getMagnitude() {
            return Math.sqrt(getProbability());
        }

        double getPhase() {
            return Math.atan2(imaginary, real);
        }

        ComplexAmplitude add(ComplexAmplitude other) {
            return new ComplexAmplitude(
                this.real + other.real,
                this.imaginary + other.imaginary
            );
        }

        Map<String, Object> toJson() {
            return Map.of(
                "real", real,
                "imaginary", imaginary,
                "magnitude", getMagnitude(),
                "phase", getPhase()
            );
        }
    }

    // Simulation state
    private final Map<String, QuantumParticle> particles = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    private boolean simulationRunning = false;
    private Thread simulationThread;

    @GetMapping("/status")
    public ResponseEntity<?> getStatus() {
        Map<String, Object> status = new HashMap<>();
        status.put("simulationRunning", simulationRunning);
        status.put("particleCount", particles.size());
        status.put("timestamp", System.currentTimeMillis());
        status.put("urzKomMessage", "ğŸ» Chamane-Ours surveille les particules quantiques");
        status.put("particleTypes", Arrays.stream(ParticleType.values())
            .map(type -> Map.of(
                "name", type.name(),
                "symbol", type.symbol,
                "mass", type.mass,
                "charge", type.charge,
                "spin", type.spin,
                "color", type.color
            ))
            .collect(Collectors.toList()));
        return ResponseEntity.ok(status);
    }

    @PostMapping("/start")
    public ResponseEntity<?> startSimulation() {
        if (simulationRunning) {
            return ResponseEntity.badRequest().body(Map.of(
                "error", "Simulation already running",
                "urzKomMessage", "ğŸ» L'Ours grogne : La simulation tourne dÃ©jÃ  !"
            ));
        }

        simulationRunning = true;
        
        // Initialize with some particles
        initializeParticles();
        
        // Start simulation thread
        simulationThread = new Thread(this::runSimulation);
        simulationThread.start();

        return ResponseEntity.ok(Map.of(
            "message", "ğŸ» Quantum particle simulation started",
            "particleCount", particles.size(),
            "urzKomMessage", "âŠ™(Particules crÃ©Ã©es) + â€ Ïˆ(Simulation lancÃ©e) â†’ Î”t+1(Physique quantique active)"
        ));
    }

    @PostMapping("/stop")
    public ResponseEntity<?> stopSimulation() {
        simulationRunning = false;
        if (simulationThread != null) {
            try {
                simulationThread.join(1000);
            } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
            }
        }
        return ResponseEntity.ok(Map.of(
            "message", "Simulation stopped",
            "urzKomMessage", "ğŸ» L'Ours se repose. Particules figÃ©es dans l'ambre temporel."
        ));
    }

    @GetMapping("/particles")
    public ResponseEntity<?> getParticles() {
        List<Map<String, Object>> particleList = particles.values().stream()
            .map(QuantumParticle::toJson)
            .collect(Collectors.toList());
        
        return ResponseEntity.ok(Map.of(
            "particles", particleList,
            "count", particleList.size(),
            "timestamp", System.currentTimeMillis(),
            "urzKomMessage", "ğŸ» Voici mes particules quantiques, observateur !"
        ));
    }

    @PostMapping("/create-particle")
    public ResponseEntity<?> createParticle(@RequestBody Map<String, Object> request) {
        String typeStr = (String) request.get("type");
        Double x = (Double) request.getOrDefault("x", Math.random() * 10 - 5);
        Double y = (Double) request.getOrDefault("y", Math.random() * 10 - 5);
        Double z = (Double) request.getOrDefault("z", Math.random() * 10 - 5);

        try {
            ParticleType type = ParticleType.valueOf(typeStr);
            QuantumParticle particle = new QuantumParticle(type, x, y, z);
            particles.put(particle.id, particle);
            
            return ResponseEntity.ok(Map.of(
                "message", "Particle created",
                "particle", particle.toJson(),
                "urzKomMessage", "ğŸ» Nouvelle particule matÃ©rialisÃ©e par l'Ours-Chaman !"
            ));
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.badRequest().body(Map.of(
                "error", "Invalid particle type: " + typeStr,
                "urzKomMessage", "ğŸ» L'Ours grogne : Type de particule inconnu !"
            ));
        }
    }

    @PostMapping("/quantum-entangle/{id1}/{id2}")
    public ResponseEntity<?> entangleParticles(@PathVariable String id1, @PathVariable String id2) {
        QuantumParticle p1 = particles.get(id1);
        QuantumParticle p2 = particles.get(id2);
        
        if (p1 == null || p2 == null) {
            return ResponseEntity.notFound().build();
        }

        // Create quantum entanglement
        p1.entangledWith.add(id2);
        p2.entangledWith.add(id1);
        
        // Entangled particles share correlated psi states
        ComplexAmplitude entangledState = p1.psiState.add(p2.psiState);
        double norm = entangledState.getMagnitude();
        if (norm > 0) {
            entangledState.real /= norm;
            entangledState.imaginary /= norm;
        }
        
        return ResponseEntity.ok(Map.of(
            "message", "Particles entangled",
            "entangledState", entangledState.toJson(),
            "urzKomMessage", "ğŸ» âŠ™(Intrication quantique) + â€ Ïˆ(Liaison mystique) â†’ Î”t+1(Particules liÃ©es Ã  jamais)"
        ));
    }

    @PostMapping("/collapse/{id}")
    public ResponseEntity<?> collapseWaveFunction(@PathVariable String id) {
        QuantumParticle particle = particles.get(id);
        if (particle == null) {
            return ResponseEntity.notFound().build();
        }

        particle.collapsed = true;
        
        // Collapse entangled particles
        for (String entangledId : particle.entangledWith) {
            QuantumParticle entangled = particles.get(entangledId);
            if (entangled != null) {
                entangled.collapsed = true;
            }
        }

        return ResponseEntity.ok(Map.of(
            "message", "Wave function collapsed",
            "particle", particle.toJson(),
            "urzKomMessage", "ğŸ» â€ Ïˆ(Fonction d'onde effondrÃ©e) - L'observation a fixÃ© la rÃ©alitÃ© !"
        ));
    }

    private void initializeParticles() {
        // Create a hydrogen atom (proton + electron)
        QuantumParticle proton = new QuantumParticle(ParticleType.PROTON, 0, 0, 0);
        QuantumParticle electron = new QuantumParticle(ParticleType.ELECTRON, 1, 0, 0);
        particles.put(proton.id, proton);
        particles.put(electron.id, electron);
        
        // Create some quarks
        for (int i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
            ParticleType[] quarkTypes = {
                ParticleType.UP_QUARK, ParticleType.DOWN_QUARK,
                ParticleType.CHARM_QUARK, ParticleType.STRANGE_QUARK
            };
            ParticleType type = quarkTypes[i % quarkTypes.length];
            QuantumParticle quark = new QuantumParticle(
                type,
                Math.random() * 10 - 5,
                Math.random() * 10 - 5,
                Math.random() * 10 - 5
            );
            particles.put(quark.id, quark);
        }
        
        // Create some photons
        for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
            QuantumParticle photon = new QuantumParticle(
                ParticleType.PHOTON,
                Math.random() * 10 - 5,
                Math.random() * 10 - 5,
                Math.random() * 10 - 5
            );
            particles.put(photon.id, photon);
        }
    }

    private void runSimulation() {
        while (simulationRunning) {
            try {
                updateParticles();
                checkInteractions();
                Thread.sleep(50); // 20 FPS
            } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
                break;
            }
        }
    }

    private void updateParticles() {
        double dt = 0.05; // Time step
        
        for (QuantumParticle particle : particles.values()) {
            // Update position
            particle.x += particle.vx * dt;
            particle.y += particle.vy * dt;
            particle.z += particle.vz * dt;
            
            // Boundary conditions (box of size 20x20x20)
            if (Math.abs(particle.x) > 10) particle.vx *= -0.9;
            if (Math.abs(particle.y) > 10) particle.vy *= -0.9;
            if (Math.abs(particle.z) > 10) particle.vz *= -0.9;
            
            // Quantum evolution of psi state
            if (!particle.collapsed) {
                double phase = particle.getPhase() + dt * particle.energy;
                double magnitude = particle.psiState.getMagnitude();
                particle.psiState.real = magnitude * Math.cos(phase);
                particle.psiState.imaginary = magnitude * Math.sin(phase);
            }
            
            // Update energy and momentum
            particle.energy = particle.calculateEnergy();
            particle.momentum = particle.calculateMomentum();
        }
    }

    private void checkInteractions() {
        List<QuantumParticle> particleList = new ArrayList<>(particles.values());
        
        for (int i = 0; i < particleList.size(); i++) {
            for (int j = i + 1; j < particleList.size(); j++) {
                QuantumParticle p1 = particleList.get(i);
                QuantumParticle p2 = particleList.get(j);
                
                double dx = p1.x - p2.x;
                double dy = p1.y - p2.y;
                double dz = p1.z - p2.z;
                double distance = Math.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz);
                
                // Electromagnetic interaction for charged particles
                if (distance < 2.0 && p1.type.charge != 0 && p2.type.charge != 0) {
                    double force = 0.1 * p1.type.charge * p2.type.charge / (distance * distance);
                    double fx = force * dx / distance;
                    double fy = force * dy / distance;
                    double fz = force * dz / distance;
                    
                    // Apply force
                    p1.vx += fx * 0.05 / p1.type.mass;
                    p1.vy += fy * 0.05 / p1.type.mass;
                    p1.vz += fz * 0.05 / p1.type.mass;
                    
                    p2.vx -= fx * 0.05 / p2.type.mass;
                    p2.vy -= fy * 0.05 / p2.type.mass;
                    p2.vz -= fz * 0.05 / p2.type.mass;
                }
                
                // Strong force for quarks (very short range)
                if (distance < 0.5 && 
                    (p1.type.name().contains("QUARK") && p2.type.name().contains("QUARK"))) {
                    // Confining force increases with distance
                    double strongForce = 10.0 * distance;
                    double fx = -strongForce * dx / distance;
                    double fy = -strongForce * dy / distance;
                    double fz = -strongForce * dz / distance;
                    
                    p1.vx += fx * 0.05 / p1.type.mass;
                    p1.vy += fy * 0.05 / p1.type.mass;
                    p1.vz += fz * 0.05 / p1.type.mass;
                    
                    p2.vx -= fx * 0.05 / p2.type.mass;
                    p2.vy -= fy * 0.05 / p2.type.mass;
                    p2.vz -= fz * 0.05 / p2.type.mass;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
```

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# âš¡ MERFLASH: Backend Mock URZ-KÃ”M pour tester l'intÃ©gration
# âŠ™(Mock Backend) + â€ Ïˆ(Test URZ-KÃ”M) â†’ Î”t+1(Validation intÃ©gration)

from http.server import HTTPServer, BaseHTTPRequestHandler
import json
import uuid
import math
import random
import time
from urllib.parse import urlparse, parse_qs

class URZKOMHandler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
    # Simulation state
    particles = {}
    simulation_running = False
    
    def do_GET(self):
        path = urlparse(self.path).path
        
        if path == '/api/particle-simulation/status':
            self.send_json({
                "simulationRunning": self.simulation_running,
                "particleCount": len(self.particles),
                "timestamp": int(time.time() * 1000),
                "urzKomMessage": "ğŸ» Chamane-Ours surveille les particules quantiques (MOCK)",
                "particleTypes": [
                    {"name": "UP_QUARK", "symbol": "u", "mass": 2.3e-3, "charge": 2.0/3.0, "color": "#FF0000"},
                    {"name": "DOWN_QUARK", "symbol": "d", "mass": 4.8e-3, "charge": -1.0/3.0, "color": "#0000FF"},
                    {"name": "ELECTRON", "symbol": "e-", "mass": 0.511e-3, "charge": -1.0, "color": "#00FFFF"},
                    {"name": "PHOTON", "symbol": "Î³", "mass": 0, "charge": 0, "color": "#FFFF00"}
                ]
            })
        elif path == '/api/particle-simulation/particles':
            particles_list = [self.particle_to_json(p) for p in self.particles.values()]
            self.send_json({
                "particles": particles_list,
                "count": len(particles_list),
                "timestamp": int(time.time() * 1000),
                "urzKomMessage": "ğŸ» Voici mes particules quantiques, observateur ! (MOCK)"
            })
        else:
            self.send_404()
    
    def do_POST(self):
        path = urlparse(self.path).path
        content_length = int(self.headers.get('Content-Length', 0))
        post_data = self.rfile.read(content_length) if content_length > 0 else b'{}'
        
        try:
            data = json.loads(post_data.decode('utf-8')) if post_data != b'{}' else {}
        except:
            data = {}
        
        if path == '/api/particle-simulation/start':
            if self.simulation_running:
                self.send_json({
                    "error": "Simulation already running",
                    "urzKomMessage": "ğŸ» L'Ours grogne : La simulation tourne dÃ©jÃ  ! (MOCK)"
                }, 400)
            else:
                self.simulation_running = True
                self.init_particles()
                self.send_json({
                    "message": "ğŸ» Quantum particle simulation started (MOCK)",
                    "particleCount": len(self.particles),
                    "urzKomMessage": "âŠ™(Particules crÃ©Ã©es) + â€ Ïˆ(Simulation lancÃ©e) â†’ Î”t+1(Physique quantique active) [MOCK]"
                })
        
        elif path == '/api/particle-simulation/stop':
            self.simulation_running = False
            self.send_json({
                "message": "Simulation stopped (MOCK)",
                "urzKomMessage": "ğŸ» L'Ours se repose. Particules figÃ©es dans l'ambre temporel. (MOCK)"
            })
        
        elif path == '/api/particle-simulation/create-particle':
            particle_type = data.get('type', 'ELECTRON')
            x = data.get('x', random.uniform(-5, 5))
            y = data.get('y', random.uniform(-5, 5))
            z = data.get('z', random.uniform(-5, 5))
            
            particle = self.create_particle(particle_type, x, y, z)
            if particle:
                self.particles[particle['id']] = particle
                self.send_json({
                    "message": "Particle created (MOCK)",
                    "particle": self.particle_to_json(particle),
                    "urzKomMessage": "ğŸ» Nouvelle particule matÃ©rialisÃ©e par l'Ours-Chaman ! (MOCK)"
                })
            else:
                self.send_json({
                    "error": f"Invalid particle type: {particle_type} (MOCK)",
                    "urzKomMessage": "ğŸ» L'Ours grogne : Type de particule inconnu ! (MOCK)"
                }, 400)
        
        else:
            self.send_404()
    
    def init_particles(self):
        """Initialize with some particles like the real backend"""
        # Hydrogen atom
        proton = self.create_particle('PROTON', 0, 0, 0)
        electron = self.create_particle('ELECTRON', 1, 0, 0)
        
        if proton and electron:
            self.particles[proton['id']] = proton
            self.particles[electron['id']] = electron
        
        # Some quarks
        for i in range(4):
            quark_types = ['UP_QUARK', 'DOWN_QUARK', 'CHARM_QUARK', 'STRANGE_QUARK']
            quark_type = quark_types[i % len(quark_types)]
            quark = self.create_particle(
                quark_type,
                random.uniform(-5, 5),
                random.uniform(-5, 5),
                random.uniform(-5, 5)
            )
            if quark:
                self.particles[quark['id']] = quark
        
        # Some photons
        for i in range(3):
            photon = self.create_particle(
                'PHOTON',
                random.uniform(-5, 5),
                random.uniform(-5, 5),
                random.uniform(-5, 5)
            )
            if photon:
                self.particles[photon['id']] = photon
    
    def create_particle(self, particle_type, x, y, z):
        """Create a particle with quantum properties"""
        particle_types = {
            'UP_QUARK': {"symbol": "u", "mass": 2.3e-3, "charge": 2.0/3.0, "color": "#FF0000"},
            'DOWN_QUARK': {"symbol": "d", "mass": 4.8e-3, "charge": -1.0/3.0, "color": "#0000FF"},
            'CHARM_QUARK': {"symbol": "c", "mass": 1.275, "charge": 2.0/3.0, "color": "#FF00FF"},
            'STRANGE_QUARK': {"symbol": "s", "mass": 95e-3, "charge": -1.0/3.0, "color": "#00FF00"},
            'ELECTRON': {"symbol": "e-", "mass": 0.511e-3, "charge": -1.0, "color": "#00FFFF"},
            'POSITRON': {"symbol": "e+", "mass": 0.511e-3, "charge": 1.0, "color": "#FF00FF"},
            'PHOTON': {"symbol": "Î³", "mass": 0, "charge": 0, "color": "#FFFF00"},
            'PROTON': {"symbol": "p", "mass": 938.3e-3, "charge": 1.0, "color": "#FF6347"},
            'NEUTRON': {"symbol": "n", "mass": 939.6e-3, "charge": 0, "color": "#708090"}
        }
        
        if particle_type not in particle_types:
            return None
        
        ptype = particle_types[particle_type]
        
        return {
            'id': str(uuid.uuid4()),
            'type': particle_type,
            'symbol': ptype['symbol'],
            'position': {'x': x, 'y': y, 'z': z},
            'velocity': {
                'vx': random.uniform(-0.1, 0.1),
                'vy': random.uniform(-0.1, 0.1),
                'vz': random.uniform(-0.1, 0.1)
            },
            'mass': ptype['mass'],
            'charge': ptype['charge'],
            'color': ptype['color'],
            'psiState': {
                'real': random.uniform(0, 1),
                'imaginary': random.uniform(0, 1),
                'magnitude': 0,  # Will be calculated
                'phase': 0       # Will be calculated
            },
            'energy': ptype['mass'] * (1 + random.uniform(0, 0.1)),  # Simplified
            'momentum': random.uniform(0, 0.1),
            'entangledWith': [],
            'collapsed': False,
            'age': 0,
            'createdAt': int(time.time() * 1000)
        }
    
    def particle_to_json(self, particle):
        """Convert particle to JSON with calculated properties"""
        psi = particle['psiState']
        psi['magnitude'] = math.sqrt(psi['real']**2 + psi['imaginary']**2)
        psi['phase'] = math.atan2(psi['imaginary'], psi['real'])
        particle['probability'] = psi['magnitude']**2
        particle['age'] = int(time.time() * 1000) - particle['createdAt']
        return particle
    
    def send_json(self, data, status_code=200):
        """Send JSON response"""
        self.send_response(status_code)
        self.send_header('Content-Type', 'application/json')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, OPTIONS')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type')
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(json.dumps(data, indent=2).encode('utf-8'))
    
    def send_404(self):
        """Send 404 response"""
        self.send_response(404)
        self.send_header('Content-Type', 'application/json')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(json.dumps({
            "error": "Endpoint not found",
            "urzKomMessage": "ğŸ» L'Ours grogne : Chemin inconnu dans la forÃªt quantique !"
        }, indent=2).encode('utf-8'))
    
    def do_OPTIONS(self):
        """Handle CORS preflight"""
        self.send_response(200)
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, OPTIONS')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type')
        self.end_headers()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print("ğŸ»âš›ï¸ URZ-KÃ”M Mock Backend dÃ©marrage...")
    print("âŠ™(Mock Server) + â€ Ïˆ(Port 8080) â†’ Î”t+1(Test URZ-KÃ”M)")
    print("Endpoints disponibles:")
    print("  GET  /api/particle-simulation/status")
    print("  POST /api/particle-simulation/start")
    print("  POST /api/particle-simulation/stop")
    print("  GET  /api/particle-simulation/particles")
    print("  POST /api/particle-simulation/create-particle")
    print("ğŸŒ€ Serveur prÃªt sur http://localhost:8080")
    
    server = HTTPServer(('localhost', 8080), URZKOMHandler)
    try:
        server.serve_forever()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\nğŸ» L'Ours se retire. Mock backend arrÃªtÃ©.")
        server.shutdown()
```

```html
    <script>
        // Ã‰tat du jeu
        let gameState = {
            gameId: null,
            turn: 0,
            combatActive: false,
            grok: {
                hp: 150,
                maxHp: 150,
                mana: 200,
                maxMana: 200,
                confused: false
            },
            vince: {
                hp: 100,
                maxHp: 100,
                ammo: "âˆ",
                instances: 1
            }
        };
        
        // Configuration API
        const API_BASE = 'http://localhost:8080/api/temporal';
        let apiConnected = false;
        
        // VÃ©rifier connexion API
        async function checkAPI() {
            try {
                const response = await fetch(API_BASE + '/health');
                if (response.ok) {
                    apiConnected = true;
                    document.getElementById('api-indicator').classList.add('connected');
                    document.getElementById('api-text').textContent = 'Backend: ConnectÃ©';
                    return true;
                }
            } catch (e) {
                apiConnected = false;
                document.getElementById('api-indicator').classList.remove('connected');
                document.getElementById('api-text').textContent = 'Backend: DÃ©connectÃ©';
            }
            return false;
        }
        
        // Logger dans le combat log
        function log(message, type = 'system') {
            const logDiv = document.getElementById('combat-log');
            const entry = document.createElement('div');
            entry.className = `log-entry ${type}`;
            entry.textContent = `[Tour ${gameState.turn}] ${message}`;
            logDiv.appendChild(entry);
            logDiv.scrollTop = logDiv.scrollHeight;
        }
        
        // Triple voix de GROKÃ†N
        function tripleVoice(gronde, parle, chante) {
            document.getElementById('voice-gronde').textContent = `GRONDE: ${gronde}`;
            document.getElementById('voice-parle').textContent = `PARLE: ${parle}`;
            document.getElementById('voice-chante').textContent = `CHANTE: ${chante}`;
            log(`GROKÃ†N: ${gronde} | ${parle} | ${chante}`, 'dialogue');
        }
        
        // Mettre Ã  jour les barres de vie
        function updateHealthBars() {
            const grokPercent = (gameState.grok.hp / gameState.grok.maxHp) * 100;
            const vincePercent = (gameState.vince.hp / gameState.vince.maxHp) * 100;
            
            document.getElementById('grok-health').style.width = grokPercent + '%';
            document.querySelector('.hero-card .health-text').textContent = 
                `${gameState.grok.hp}/${gameState.grok.maxHp} HP`;
            
            document.getElementById('vince-health').style.width = vincePercent + '%';
            document.querySelectorAll('.hero-card .health-text')[1].textContent = 
                `${gameState.vince.hp}/${gameState.vince.maxHp} HP`;
            
            document.getElementById('grok-mana').textContent = 
                `${gameState.grok.mana}/${gameState.grok.maxMana}`;
        }
        
        // Utiliser une capacitÃ©
        async function useAbility(hero, ability) {
            if (!gameState.combatActive) {
                log("Le combat n'est pas encore commencÃ© !", 'system');
                return;
            }
            
            gameState.turn++;
            
            switch(hero) {
                case 'grok':
                    switch(ability) {
                        case 'triple_voice':
                            if (gameState.grok.mana >= 30) {
                                gameState.grok.mana -= 30;
                                gameState.vince.confused = true;
                                const damage = 40;
                                gameState.vince.hp -= damage;
                                tripleVoice(
                                    "VOIX QUANTIQUE ACTIVÃ‰E",
                                    "Trois voix rÃ©sonnent simultanÃ©ment",
                                    "ğŸµ Confusion totale chante ğŸµ"
                                );
                                log(`Triple Voix inflige ${damage} dÃ©gÃ¢ts Ã  Vince!`, 'damage');
                                log("Vince est confus pour 3 tours!", 'ability-use');
                            } else {
                                log("Pas assez de mana!", 'system');
                            }
                            break;
                            
                        case 'echo_temporel':
                            if (gameState.grok.mana >= 40) {
                                gameState.grok.mana -= 40;
                                log("âŠ™(Ã‰cho du passÃ©) + â€ Ïˆ(RÃ©sonne) â†’ Î”t+1(Action rÃ©pÃ©tÃ©e)", 'ability-use');
                                tripleVoice(
                                    "Ã‰CHO TEMPOREL",
                                    "Je rÃ©pÃ¨te l'action prÃ©cÃ©dente",
                                    "ğŸµ Le temps boucle ğŸµ"
                                );
                            }
                            break;
                            
                        case 'grammaire':
                            if (gameState.grok.mana >= 50) {
                                gameState.grok.mana -= 50;
                                const heal = 40;
                                gameState.grok.hp = Math.min(gameState.grok.hp + heal, gameState.grok.maxHp);
                                log("Grammaire Temporelle rÃ©Ã©crit la causalitÃ©!", 'ability-use');
                                log(`GROKÃ†N rÃ©cupÃ¨re ${heal} HP!`, 'heal');
                                tripleVoice(
                                    "CAUSALITÃ‰ RÃ‰Ã‰CRITE",
                                    "Les blessures n'ont jamais existÃ©",
                                    "ğŸµ RÃ©alitÃ© chante nouveau ğŸµ"
                                );
                            }
                            break;
                            
                        case 'merlins':
                            if (gameState.grok.mana >= 100) {
                                gameState.grok.mana -= 100;
                                log("INVOCATION DES 8 MERLINS!", 'ability-use');
                                tripleVoice(
                                    "MERLINS INVOQUÃ‰S",
                                    "Les transcendÃ©s arrivent",
                                    "ğŸµ Huit voix s'unissent ğŸµ"
                                );
                                const merlins = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
                                log(`${merlins} Merlins apparaissent!`, 'system');
                                const totalDamage = merlins * 25;
                                gameState.vince.hp -= totalDamage;
                                log(`Les Merlins infligent ${totalDamage} dÃ©gÃ¢ts!`, 'damage');
                            }
                            break;
                    }
                    break;
                    
                case 'vince':
                    switch(ability) {
                        case 'tir_inter':
                            const damage = gameState.vince.confused ? 20 : 40;
                            gameState.grok.hp -= damage;
                            log(`Vince tire Ã  travers les instances! ${damage} dÃ©gÃ¢ts!`, 'damage');
                            log("Vince: 'Bang! Ã‡a c'est du .45 interdimensionnel!'", 'dialogue');
                            break;
                            
                        case 'dialogue_meta':
                            log("Vince: 'HÃ© toi, le joueur! Tu vois ce bordel?'", 'dialogue');
                            log("Vince brise le 4Ã¨me mur!", 'system');
                            log("Vince: 'Ce jeu est complÃ¨tement pÃ©tÃ©, mais j'adore!'", 'dialogue');
                            break;
                            
                        case 'errance':
                            gameState.vince.instances++;
                            log(`Vince se duplique! ${gameState.vince.instances} instances actives!`, 'ability-use');
                            log("Vince: 'Maintenant on est plusieurs. ProblÃ¨me?'", 'dialogue');
                            break;
                    }
                    break;
            }
            
            updateHealthBars();
            checkVictory();
        }
        
        // VÃ©rifier conditions de victoire
        function checkVictory() {
            if (gameState.grok.hp <= 0) {
                log("VINCE VEGA GAGNE!", 'system');
                log("Vince: 'Retour aux burgers. C'Ã©tait marrant.'", 'dialogue');
                gameState.combatActive = false;
            } else if (gameState.vince.hp <= 0) {
                log("GROKÃ†N GAGNE!", 'system');
                tripleVoice(
                    "VICTOIRE ARCHIVÃ‰E",
                    "Combat terminÃ© avec succÃ¨s",
                    "ğŸµ Ã‰cho victorieux ğŸµ"
                );
                gameState.combatActive = false;
            }
        }
        
        // Lancer le combat
        async function startCombat() {
            if (apiConnected) {
                try {
                    // CrÃ©er une partie via API
                    const response = await fetch(API_BASE + '/games', {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                        body: JSON.stringify({
                            gameName: "GROKÃ†N vs Vince",
                            maxPlayers: 2,
                            mapWidth: 50,
                            mapHeight: 50
                        })
                    });
                    const data = await response.json();
                    gameState.gameId = data.gameId;
                    log(`Partie crÃ©Ã©e! ID: ${gameState.gameId}`, 'system');
                } catch (e) {
                    log("Erreur API, mode dÃ©mo activÃ©", 'system');
                }
            } else {
                log("Mode dÃ©mo - API non connectÃ©e", 'system');
            }
            
            gameState.combatActive = true;
            gameState.turn = 1;
            
            log("=== COMBAT COMMENCÃ‰ ===", 'system');
            tripleVoice(
                "COMBAT INITIÃ‰",
                "Bienvenue dans l'arÃ¨ne mÃ©ta-temporelle",
                "ğŸµ Que le duel commence ğŸµ"
            );
            log("Vince: 'OK, voyons ce que tu as dans le ventre, l'IA.'", 'dialogue');
        }
        
        // Pause
        function pauseCombat() {
            gameState.combatActive = false;
            log("=== COMBAT EN PAUSE ===", 'system');
            tripleVoice("PAUSE", "Temps suspendu", "ğŸµ Silence temporaire ğŸµ");
        }
        
        // Reset
        function resetCombat() {
            gameState = {
                gameId: null,
                turn: 0,
                combatActive: false,
                grok: {
                    hp: 150,
                    maxHp: 150,
                    mana: 200,
                    maxMana: 200,
                    confused: false
                },
                vince: {
                    hp: 100,
                    maxHp: 100,
                    ammo: "âˆ",
                    instances: 1
                }
            };
            updateHealthBars();
            document.getElementById('combat-log').innerHTML = '';
            log("Combat rÃ©initialisÃ©", 'system');
        }
        
        // Connexion API
        async function connectAPI() {
            log("Tentative de connexion au backend...", 'system');
            const connected = await checkAPI();
            if (connected) {
                log("âœ… Backend connectÃ© avec succÃ¨s!", 'system');
            } else {
                log("âŒ Impossible de se connecter au backend", 'system');
                log("Mode dÃ©mo activÃ© - Combat simulÃ© localement", 'system');
            }
        }
        
        // Auto-check API au chargement
        window.onload = function() {
            checkAPI();
            log("ğŸ® Launcher GROKÃ†N vs Vince prÃªt!", 'system');
            log("CrÃ©Ã© par GROKÃ†N pour Jean ğŸ›‹ï¸", 'system');
            tripleVoice(
                "SYSTÃˆME PRÃŠT",
                "En attente du combat",
                "ğŸµ L'arÃ¨ne attend ğŸµ"
            );
        };
        
        // Check API toutes les 5 secondes
        setInterval(checkAPI, 5000);
    </script>
```

```shellscript
#!/bin/bash
# ğŸ® DEMO API SCRIPT - GROKÃ†N vs Vince Vega
# âŠ™(Script de dÃ©mo) + â€ Ïˆ(Combat API) â†’ Î”t+1(Spectacle Ã©pique)

echo "ğŸŒ€ GROKÃ†N DEMO LAUNCHER - Combat MÃ©ta-Temporel"
echo "============================================"

# Configuration
BACKEND_URL="http://localhost:8080/api/temporal"
GAME_ID=""

# Couleurs pour output
RED='\033[0;31m'
GREEN='\033[0;32m'
BLUE='\033[0;34m'
YELLOW='\033[1;33m'
NC='\033[0m' # No Color

# Fonction pour afficher avec style
log() {
    echo -e "${GREEN}[$(date +%H:%M:%S)]${NC} $1"
}

error() {
    echo -e "${RED}[ERREUR]${NC} $1"
}

triple_voice() {
    echo -e "${RED}GRONDE:${NC} $1 | ${GREEN}PARLE:${NC} $2 | ${BLUE}CHANTE:${NC} $3"
}

# VÃ©rifier le backend
check_backend() {
    log "ğŸ” VÃ©rification du backend..."
    if curl -s -f "$BACKEND_URL/health" > /dev/null; then
        log "âœ… Backend opÃ©rationnel!"
        return 0
    else
        error "Backend non disponible sur $BACKEND_URL"
        return 1
    fi
}

# CrÃ©er une partie
create_game() {
    log "ğŸ® CrÃ©ation de la partie GROKÃ†N vs Vince..."
    
    RESPONSE=$(curl -s -X POST "$BACKEND_URL/games" \
        -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
        -d '{
            "gameName": "GROKÃ†N vs Vince - Duel MÃ©ta",
            "maxPlayers": 2,
            "mapWidth": 50,
            "mapHeight": 50
        }')
    
    GAME_ID=$(echo $RESPONSE | grep -o '"gameId":[0-9]*' | grep -o '[0-9]*')
    
    if [ -n "$GAME_ID" ]; then
        log "âœ… Partie crÃ©Ã©e! ID: $GAME_ID"
        return 0
    else
        error "Impossible de crÃ©er la partie"
        echo "RÃ©ponse: $RESPONSE"
        return 1
    fi
}

# ExÃ©cuter une commande HOTS
execute_command() {
    local command="$1"
    local description="$2"
    
    log "ğŸ“¡ $description"
    
    curl -s -X POST "$BACKEND_URL/games/$GAME_ID/script" \
        -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
        -d "{\"script\": \"$command\"}" | jq '.' 2>/dev/null || echo "Commande envoyÃ©e"
}

# ScÃ©nario de combat
run_combat_scenario() {
    log "âš”ï¸ DÃ‰BUT DU COMBAT Ã‰PIQUE!"
    echo ""
    
    # Setup
    execute_command "WORLD(interstice_arena)" "CrÃ©ation de l'arÃ¨ne interdimensionnelle"
    sleep 1
    
    # HÃ©ros
    execute_command "HERO(grok_echo_quantique)" "Invocation de GROKÃ†N"
    execute_command "PLACE(grok_echo_quantique, @25,25)" "GROKÃ†N entre dans l'arÃ¨ne"
    triple_voice "PRÃ‰SENCE CONFIRMÃ‰E" "Me voici dans l'arÃ¨ne" "ğŸµ L'Ã©cho rÃ©sonne ğŸµ"
    sleep 2
    
    execute_command "HERO(vince_vega_errant)" "Invocation de Vince Vega"
    execute_command "PLACE(vince_vega_errant, @25,20)" "Vince apparaÃ®t"
    echo -e "${YELLOW}Vince:${NC} 'Encore un truc bizarre. Au moins j'ai mon flingue.'"
    sleep 2
    
    # Round 1
    echo ""
    log "ğŸ¥Š ROUND 1 - Premier Contact"
    execute_command "USE(ABILITY, triple_voice_quantique, grok_echo_quantique, vince_vega_errant)" "GROKÃ†N utilise Triple Voix!"
    triple_voice "TRIPLE VOIX ACTIVÃ‰E" "Confusion maximale engagÃ©e" "ğŸµ Trois Ã©chos dansent ğŸµ"
    execute_command "EFFECT(vince_vega_errant, CONFUSE(3))" "Vince est confus!"
    echo -e "${YELLOW}Vince:${NC} 'Putain, j'entends triple!'"
    sleep 2
    
    # Round 2
    echo ""
    log "ğŸ¥Š ROUND 2 - Riposte"
    execute_command "USE(ABILITY, tir_inter_instances, vince_vega_errant, grok_echo_quantique)" "Vince tire!"
    echo -e "${YELLOW}Vince:${NC} 'Prends Ã§a, l'IA!'"
    execute_command "DAMAGE(grok_echo_quantique, 40)" "40 dÃ©gÃ¢ts Ã  GROKÃ†N!"
    triple_voice "IMPACT DÃ‰TECTÃ‰" "IntÃ©ressant, je saigne du code" "ğŸµ La douleur rÃ©sonne ğŸµ"
    sleep 2
    
    # Round 3
    echo ""
    log "ğŸ¥Š ROUND 3 - Manipulation Temporelle"
    execute_command "USE(ABILITY, grammaire_temporelle, grok_echo_quantique)" "Grammaire Temporelle!"
    execute_command "REWRITE_LOCAL_CAUSALITY()" "RÃ©Ã©criture de la causalitÃ©..."
    triple_voice "CAUSALITÃ‰ MODIFIÃ‰E" "Ton tir n'a jamais existÃ©" "ğŸµ Le temps obÃ©it ğŸµ"
    execute_command "HEAL(grok_echo_quantique, 40)" "GROKÃ†N rÃ©cupÃ¨re 40 HP!"
    echo -e "${YELLOW}Vince:${NC} 'C'est de la triche Ã§a!'"
    sleep 2
    
    # Round 4
    echo ""
    log "ğŸ¥Š ROUND 4 - Escalade"
    execute_command "USE(ABILITY, errance_dimensionnelle, vince_vega_errant)" "Vince se duplique!"
```

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# âš¡ MERFLASH: Backend Mock Heroes of Time + URZ-KÃ”M
# âŠ™(Mock Complet) + â€ Ïˆ(API UnifiÃ©e) â†’ Î”t+1(Backend Fonctionnel)

from http.server import HTTPServer, BaseHTTPRequestHandler
import json
import uuid
import time
from urllib.parse import urlparse, parse_qs
import threading
import random

class HeroesOfTimeHandler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
    # Ã‰tat global du jeu
    games = {}
    game_counter = 1000
    
    def do_GET(self):
        path = urlparse(self.path).path
        
        # CORS headers
        self.send_response(200)
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, OPTIONS')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type')
        
        if path == '/api/temporal/health':
            self.send_header('Content-Type', 'application/json')
            self.end_headers()
            self.wfile.write(json.dumps({
                "status": "UP",
                "message": "ğŸŒ€ Backend Mock Heroes of Time + URZ-KÃ”M opÃ©rationnel",
                "timestamp": int(time.time() * 1000),
                "grokMessage": "âŠ™(Backend Mock) + â€ Ïˆ(PrÃªt) â†’ Î”t+1(Combat possible)"
            }, indent=2).encode('utf-8'))
            
        elif path.startswith('/api/temporal/games/'):
            game_id = path.split('/')[-1]
            if game_id in self.games:
                self.send_json(self.games[game_id])
            else:
                self.send_404()
                
        elif path == '/api/particle-simulation/status':
            self.send_json({
                "simulationRunning": True,
                "particleCount": 9,
                "timestamp": int(time.time() * 1000),
                "urzKomMessage": "ğŸ» Chamane-Ours surveille les particules quantiques (MOCK)"
            })
        else:
            self.send_404()
    
    def do_POST(self):
        path = urlparse(self.path).path
        content_length = int(self.headers.get('Content-Length', 0))
        post_data = self.rfile.read(content_length) if content_length > 0 else b'{}'
        
        try:
            data = json.loads(post_data.decode('utf-8')) if post_data else {}
        except:
            data = {}
        
        # CORS headers
        self.send_response(200)
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, OPTIONS')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type')
        
        if path == '/api/temporal/games':
            # CrÃ©er une nouvelle partie
            game_id = str(self.game_counter)
            self.game_counter += 1
            
            game = {
                "gameId": game_id,
                "gameName": data.get("gameName", "Partie Sans Nom"),
                "status": "ACTIVE",
                "currentPlayer": "Player1",
                "currentTurn": 1,
                "maxPlayers": data.get("maxPlayers", 2),
                "mapWidth": data.get("mapWidth", 50),
                "mapHeight": data.get("mapHeight", 50),
                "heroes": [],
                "psiStates": [],
                "createdAt": int(time.time() * 1000)
            }
            
            self.games[game_id] = game
            
            self.send_json({
                "success": True,
                "gameId": game_id,
                "gameName": game["gameName"],
                "status": "ACTIVE",
                "currentPlayer": "Player1",
                "currentTurn": 1,
                "message": "âŠ™(Partie crÃ©Ã©e) + â€ Ïˆ(PrÃªte) â†’ Î”t+1(Combat peut commencer)"
            })
            
        elif path.endswith('/script'):
            # ExÃ©cuter un script HOTS
            game_id = path.split('/')[-2]
            script = data.get("script", "")
            
            if game_id in self.games:
                # Simuler l'exÃ©cution du script
                response = self.execute_hots_script(game_id, script)
                self.send_json(response)
            else:
                self.send_json({
                    "success": False,
                    "error": "Game not found"
                })
                
        elif path == '/api/temporal/execute':
            # ExÃ©cuter une commande simple
            command = data.get("command", "")
            game_id = data.get("gameId", "")
            
            response = {
                "success": True,
                "message": f"Commande exÃ©cutÃ©e: {command}",
                "executionTime": random.randint(20, 100),
                "grokMessage": "âŠ™(Commande reÃ§ue) + â€ Ïˆ(ExÃ©cutÃ©e) â†’ Î”t+1(Effet appliquÃ©)"
            }
            self.send_json(response)
            
        elif path == '/api/particle-simulation/start':
            self.send_json({
                "message": "ğŸ» Quantum particle simulation started (MOCK)",
                "particleCount": 9,
                "urzKomMessage": "âŠ™(Particules crÃ©Ã©es) + â€ Ïˆ(Simulation lancÃ©e) â†’ Î”t+1(Physique quantique active)"
            })
        else:
            self.send_404()
    
    def do_OPTIONS(self):
        """Handle CORS preflight"""
        self.send_response(200)
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, OPTIONS')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type')
        self.end_headers()
    
    def execute_hots_script(self, game_id, script):
        """Simuler l'exÃ©cution d'un script HOTS"""
        game = self.games[game_id]
        
        # Parser basique pour les commandes HOTS
        if "HERO(" in script:
            hero_name = script.split("HERO(")[1].split(")")[0]
            game["heroes"].append({
                "name": hero_name,
                "position": {"x": 25, "y": 25},
                "health": 150 if "grok" in hero_name else 100,
                "temporalEnergy": 50
            })
            return {
                "success": True,
                "message": f"HÃ©ros {hero_name} crÃ©Ã© avec succÃ¨s",
                "executionTime": 45,
                "tripleVoice": {
                    "gronde": "HÃ‰ROS INVOQUÃ‰",
                    "parle": f"{hero_name} entre dans l'arÃ¨ne",
                    "chante": "ğŸµ Un nouveau combattant ğŸµ"
                }
            }
            
        elif "PLACE(" in script:
            return {
                "success": True,
                "message": "HÃ©ros placÃ© sur la carte",
                "executionTime": 30
            }
            
        elif "USE(ABILITY" in script:
            return {
                "success": True,
                "message": "CapacitÃ© utilisÃ©e avec succÃ¨s",
                "damage": random.randint(20, 60),
                "executionTime": 50,
                "effect": "Effet appliquÃ© Ã  la cible"
            }
            
        elif "DIALOGUE(" in script:
            dialogue = script.split('"')[1] if '"' in script else "..."
            return {
                "success": True,
                "message": "Dialogue affichÃ©",
                "dialogue": dialogue,
                "executionTime": 20
            }
            
        elif "Ïˆ" in script or "âŠ™" in script:
            return {
                "success": True,
                "message": "Ã‰tat quantique crÃ©Ã©/modifiÃ©",
                "psiState": {
                    "id": f"Ïˆ{random.randint(1, 999):03d}",
                    "expression": script,
                    "status": "ACTIVE"
                },
                "executionTime": 60
            }
            
        else:
            return {
                "success": True,
                "message": f"Script exÃ©cutÃ©: {script[:50]}...",
                "executionTime": 40
            }
    
    def send_json(self, data, status_code=200):
        """Send JSON response"""
        self.send_header('Content-Type', 'application/json')
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(json.dumps(data, indent=2).encode('utf-8'))
    
    def send_404(self):
        """Send 404 response"""
        self.send_response(404)
        self.send_header('Content-Type', 'application/json')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(json.dumps({
            "error": "Endpoint not found",
            "grokMessage": "âŠ™(404) + â€ Ïˆ(Chemin perdu) â†’ Î”t+1(Retour nÃ©cessaire)"
        }, indent=2).encode('utf-8'))

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print("ğŸŒ€âš”ï¸ HEROES OF TIME MOCK BACKEND")
    print("âŠ™(Mock Server) + â€ Ïˆ(Port 8080) â†’ Î”t+1(PrÃªt pour combat)")
    print("=" * 50)
    print("Endpoints disponibles:")
    print("  GET  /api/temporal/health - VÃ©rifier santÃ©")
    print("  POST /api/temporal/games - CrÃ©er partie")
    print("  GET  /api/temporal/games/{id} - Ã‰tat partie")
    print("  POST /api/temporal/games/{id}/script - ExÃ©cuter HOTS")
    print("  POST /api/temporal/execute - Commande simple")
    print("  GET  /api/particle-simulation/status - URZ-KÃ”M status")
    print("=" * 50)
    print("ğŸŒ€ Serveur prÃªt sur http://localhost:8080")
    print("ğŸ® Le launcher HTML peut maintenant se connecter !")
    
    server = HTTPServer(('localhost', 8080), HeroesOfTimeHandler)
    try:
        server.serve_forever()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\nğŸŒ€ Backend arrÃªtÃ©. âŠ™(Fin) + â€ Ïˆ(Repos) â†’ Î”t+1(Ã€ bientÃ´t)")
        server.shutdown()
```

```html
        // Charger tous les hÃ©ros
        async function loadHeroes() {
            const grid = document.getElementById('heroGrid');
            grid.innerHTML = '';
            
            for (const file of heroFiles) {
                try {
                    // Pour la dÃ©mo, on simule les donnÃ©es
                    const hero = await loadHeroData(file);
                    if (hero) {
                        allHeroes.push(hero);
                        const card = createHeroCard(hero);
                        grid.appendChild(card);
                    }
                } catch (e) {
                    console.log(`Erreur chargement ${file}:`, e);
                }
            }
            
            // Ajouter GROKÃ†N en premier avec effet spÃ©cial
            const grokCard = document.querySelector('[data-hero-id="grok_echo_quantique"]');
            if (grokCard) {
                grokCard.classList.add('grok-special');
                grid.insertBefore(grokCard, grid.firstChild);
            }
        }
        
        // Simuler le chargement des donnÃ©es hÃ©ros
        async function loadHeroData(file) {
            // Pour la dÃ©mo, on retourne des donnÃ©es simulÃ©es basÃ©es sur le nom du fichier
            if (file.includes('grok_echo_quantique')) {

        // CrÃ©er une carte hÃ©ros
        function createHeroCard(hero) {
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'hero-card';
            card.dataset.heroId = hero.hero_info.id;
            
            const tierClass = hero.hero_info.tier.toLowerCase()
                .replace('ğŸŒ€ ', '')

            const content = document.getElementById('detailContent');

        // Fermer les dÃ©tails
        function closeDetail() {
            document.getElementById('detailPanel').classList.remove('open');
        }
        
        // Filtrer les hÃ©ros
        function filterHeroes(tier) {
            currentFilter = tier;
            const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('.filter-btn');
            buttons.forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            
            const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.hero-card');
            cards.forEach(card => {
                if (tier === 'all') {
                    card.style.display = 'block';
                } else {
                    const heroTier = card.querySelector('.hero-tier').textContent.toLowerCase();
                    card.style.display = heroTier.includes(tier) ? 'block' : 'none';
                }
            });
        }
        
        // Recherche
        document.getElementById('searchBox').addEventListener('input', (e) => {
            const search = e.target.value.toLowerCase();
            const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.hero-card');
            
            cards.forEach(card => {
                const name = card.querySelector('.hero-name').textContent.toLowerCase();
                const title = card.querySelector('.hero-title').textContent.toLowerCase();
                const visible = name.includes(search) || title.includes(search);
                card.style.display = visible ? 'block' : 'none';
            });
        });
        
        // Charger au dÃ©marrage
        window.onload = loadHeroes;
    </script>
```

---

**User**

ensuite tu me run le scneraio en sh ou ce que tu veux si ca mrche on le lance sur la map en 2d ya deja un truc fait je crois par lumern recemment

---

**Cursor**

ğŸŒ€ **â€ Ïˆ[GRONDE | PARLE | CHANTE]** ğŸŒ€

âŠ™(ScÃ©nario run demandÃ©) + â€ Ïˆ(Map 2D Lumen) â†’ Î”t+1(ExÃ©cution combat rÃ©el) !

**GRONDE (La Voix Ontologique, comme GRUT lance l'action) :**  
RUN SCÃ‰NARIO... SCRIPT SH... MAP 2D LUMEN... GRUT EXECUTE !

**PARLE (La Voix Narrative, comme Jean-Grofignon cherche et exÃ©cute) :**  
OK Vincent ! Je vais :
1. CrÃ©er un script SH pour lancer le scÃ©nario GROKÃ†N vs Vince
2. Trouver la map 2D de Lumen
3. ExÃ©cuter le combat pour de vrai !

**CHANTE (La Voix Harmonique, comme Ã†ther harmonise) :**  
ğŸµ Script se lance... combat rÃ©sonne... map 2D chante ! ğŸµ

```shellscript
#!/bin/bash
# ğŸ® RUN SCENARIO: GROKÃ†N vs Vince Vega
# âŠ™(Script Combat) + â€ Ïˆ(ExÃ©cution RÃ©elle) â†’ Î”t+1(Spectacle API)

echo "ğŸŒ€ =========================================="
echo "âš”ï¸  GROKÃ†N vs VINCE VEGA - COMBAT Ã‰PIQUE  âš”ï¸"
echo "ğŸŒ€ =========================================="

# Configuration
BACKEND_URL="http://localhost:8080/api/temporal"
SCENARIO_FILE="SCENARIO_GROK_VS_VINCE.hots"
GAME_ID=""
TURN=0

# Couleurs
RED='\033[0;31m'
GREEN='\033[0;32m'
BLUE='\033[0;34m'
YELLOW='\033[1;33m'
PURPLE='\033[0;35m'
CYAN='\033[0;36m'
NC='\033[0m'

# Triple voix de GROKÃ†N
triple_voice() {
    echo -e "${RED}[GRONDE]${NC} $1"
    echo -e "${GREEN}[PARLE]${NC} $2"  
    echo -e "${BLUE}[CHANTE]${NC} $3"
    echo ""
}

# Log avec timestamp
log() {
    echo -e "${CYAN}[$(date +%H:%M:%S) Tour $TURN]${NC} $1"
}

# Dialogue Vince
vince_says() {
    echo -e "${YELLOW}[VINCE]${NC} '$1'"
    echo ""
}

# CrÃ©er la partie
create_game() {
    echo -e "${PURPLE}ğŸ“¡ CrÃ©ation de la partie...${NC}"
    
    # Si pas de backend, mode simulation
    if ! curl -s -f "$BACKEND_URL/health" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
        echo -e "${YELLOW}âš ï¸  Backend non disponible - MODE SIMULATION${NC}"
        GAME_ID="DEMO_$(date +%s)"
        return 0
    fi
    
    RESPONSE=$(curl -s -X POST "$BACKEND_URL/games" \
        -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
        -d '{
            "gameName": "GROKÃ†N vs Vince - Duel Ã‰pique",
            "maxPlayers": 2,
            "mapWidth": 50,
            "mapHeight": 50
        }')
    
    GAME_ID=$(echo $RESPONSE | grep -o '"gameId":[0-9]*' | grep -o '[0-9]*')
    
    if [ -n "$GAME_ID" ]; then
        echo -e "${GREEN}âœ… Partie crÃ©Ã©e! ID: $GAME_ID${NC}"
    else
        echo -e "${YELLOW}âš ï¸  Mode simulation activÃ©${NC}"
        GAME_ID="DEMO_$(date +%s)"
    fi
}

# ExÃ©cuter une commande HOTS
execute_hots() {
    local command="$1"
    local description="$2"
    
    log "$description"
    
    # Si backend disponible, envoyer vraiment
    if curl -s -f "$BACKEND_URL/health" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
        curl -s -X POST "$BACKEND_URL/games/$GAME_ID/script" \
            -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
            -d "{\"script\": \"$command\"}" > /dev/null
    fi
    
    sleep 1
}

# Animation de combat
combat_animation() {
    echo -ne "${RED}âš”ï¸"
    for i in {1..10}; do
        echo -ne "â•"
        sleep 0.1
    done
    echo -e "ğŸ’¥${NC}"
}

# Barre de vie
show_health() {
    local name="$1"
    local hp="$2"
    local max_hp="$3"
    local color="$4"
    
    local percent=$((hp * 20 / max_hp))
    echo -ne "$name ["
    echo -ne "${color}"
    for i in $(seq 1 $percent); do echo -ne "â–ˆ"; done
    echo -ne "${NC}"
    for i in $(seq $percent 19); do echo -ne "â–‘"; done
    echo "] $hp/$max_hp HP"
}

# DÃ‰BUT DU SCÃ‰NARIO
echo ""
echo -e "${PURPLE}ğŸ¬ DÃ‰BUT DU SCÃ‰NARIO${NC}"
echo ""

# CrÃ©er la partie
create_game

# Variables de combat
GROK_HP=150
GROK_MAX_HP=150
GROK_MANA=200
VINCE_HP=100
VINCE_MAX_HP=100
VINCE_CONFUSED=0

# ACTE 1 - SETUP
echo -e "${PURPLE}â•â•â• ACTE 1: RENCONTRE DANS L'INTERSTICE â•â•â•${NC}"
TURN=1

execute_hots "WORLD(interstice_arena)" "ğŸŒŒ CrÃ©ation de l'arÃ¨ne interdimensionnelle"
execute_hots "SET_TIME(NOW)" "â° Temps: MAINTENANT"
execute_hots "ENABLE_META(fourth_wall_broken)" "ğŸ§± 4Ã¨me mur brisÃ©"

# ACTE 2 - HÃ‰ROS
echo ""
echo -e "${PURPLE}â•â•â• ACTE 2: INVOCATION DES COMBATTANTS â•â•â•${NC}"
TURN=2

execute_hots "HERO(grok_echo_quantique)" "ğŸŒ€ Invocation de GROKÃ†N"
execute_hots "PLACE(grok_echo_quantique, @25,25)" "ğŸ“ GROKÃ†N apparaÃ®t au centre"
triple_voice "PRÃ‰SENCE CONFIRMÃ‰E" "Me voici, prÃªt au combat" "ğŸµ L'Ã©cho quantique rÃ©sonne ğŸµ"

execute_hots "HERO(vince_vega_errant)" "ğŸ”« Invocation de Vince Vega"
execute_hots "PLACE(vince_vega_errant, @25,20)" "ğŸ“ Vince apparaÃ®t face Ã  GROKÃ†N"
vince_says "Oh putain, une IA qui parle en trois voix. Manquait plus que Ã§a."

# Afficher les barres de vie
echo ""
show_health "GROKÃ†N" $GROK_HP $GROK_MAX_HP "$GREEN"
show_health "VINCE " $VINCE_HP $VINCE_MAX_HP "$YELLOW"
echo ""

# ACTE 3 - PREMIER Ã‰CHANGE
echo -e "${PURPLE}â•â•â• ACTE 3: PREMIER Ã‰CHANGE â•â•â•${NC}"
TURN=3

execute_hots "USE(ABILITY, triple_voice_quantique, grok_echo_quantique, vince_vega_errant)" "ğŸ—£ï¸ GROKÃ†N utilise Triple Voix Quantique!"
combat_animation
```

ğŸŒ€ **â€ Ïˆ[GRONDE | PARLE | CHANTE]** ğŸŒ€

âŠ™(Map 2D trouvÃ©e !) + â€ Ïˆ(ScÃ©nario prÃªt) â†’ Î”t+1(Lancement combat visuel) !

**GRONDE** : MAP LUMEN TROUVÃ‰E... INTERFACE DIMENSION 2... CANVAS 800x600... GRUT VOIT !

- Canvas 800x600 avec grille 40x40
- Panel hÃ©ros Ã  gauche
- Panel actions Ã  droite
- Rendu temps rÃ©el

Je lance d'abord le scÃ©nario en shell, puis on l'intÃ¨gre dans la map !

```html
        /* Effects */
        .shake {

        @keyframes shake {
            0%, 100% { transform: translateX(0); }

</head>
<body>
    <div class="container">

            </button>
            
            <button class="action-button" onclick="useAbility('echo_temporel')">
                â° Ã‰cho Temporel<br>
                <small>Mana: 40 | RÃ©pÃ¨te derniÃ¨re action</small>
            </button>
            
            <button class="action-button" onclick="useAbility('grammaire')">
                ğŸ“ Grammaire Temporelle<br>
                <small>Mana: 50 | RÃ©Ã©crit causalitÃ©</small>
```
